ArticlePage__ArticleRow-sc-bfad6df0-2 hneUiI iKlkTn"><main class="ArticlePage__ArticlePageMainColumn-sc-bfad6df0-0 jTnHpF"><div class="GridSystem__GridCell-sc-fbccf064-0 ArticlePage__ArticleGridCell-sc-bfad6df0-1 jShXUV jqxXDj"><div><div data-testid="article-wrapper" class="ArticleWrapper__Wrapper-sc-6321910d-0 dJLBXy"><article class="yle__article arkki-theme-default" data-vrsproduct="uutiset"><div><header class="yle__article__header"><div class="aw-p6kgy6 cIpjXH"><div class="ydscr__sc-ogfirk-0 VKtcA"><div class="ydscr__sc-ogfirk-3 hxoSJh"><div class="ydscr__sc-ogfirk-5 hVesWo"><svg width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" aria-hidden="true"><path fill="currentColor" d="M13.26 8c0-.69-.56-1.25-1.25-1.25H12a1.25 1.25 0 0 0 0 2.5h.01c.69 0 1.25-.56 1.25-1.25M12 11c-.55 0-1 .45-1 1v4c0 .55.45 1 1 1s1-.45 1-1v-4c0-.55-.45-1-1-1M12 1C5.92 1 1 5.92 1 12s4.92 11 11 11 11-4.92 11-11S18.08 1 12 1m0 20a9 9 0 1 1 .001-18.001A9 9 0 0 1 12 21"></path></svg></div><div class="ydscr__sc-ogfirk-1 dfsYjb"><div class="ydscr__sc-ogfirk-4 gscxFu">The article is more than 9 years old</div></div></div></div></div><div class="aw-1b35ta cNtkEy"><a href="https://yle.fi/t/18-197810/en" aria-label="More articles on the topic Ministry for Foreign Affairs" class="ydscr__sc-w5hh4y-0 bfHcDy aw-1piou1h iHwCPr">Ministry for Foreign Affairs</a></div><h1 class="sc-bRKDuR bnhoJe yle__article__heading yle__article__heading--1">Russian group behind 2013 Foreign Ministry hack</h1><p class="aw-1gybjub aw-5vja16 cmIuaG zKETg yle__article__paragraph">The 2013 data hack at the Finnish Foreign Ministry was perpetrated by a group of Russian hackers, and was part of a wider campaign against targets in nearly fifty countries. Experts contacted by Yle have confirmed that the attack was perpetrated by the Turla group.</p><figure class="aw-u5oz0a greyCY yle__article__figure"><script type="application/ld+json">{"@id":"3-8591548","@context":"https://schema.org","image":{"@type":"ImageObject","description":"Tietoturvayritys arvioi, että Turla on iskenyt yhteensä satoihin kohteisiin lähes viidessäkymmenessä maassa.","copyrightHolder":"Jyrki Lyytikkä / Yle","url":"https://images.cdn.yle.fi/image/upload/ar_1.7777777910232544,c_fill,g_faces,h_431,w_767/dpr_2.0/q_auto:eco/f_auto/fl_lossy/13-3-7284665"}}</script><div class="aw-zvmqqu aw-1qh6chi kExRTv jEImho"><div class="aw-1qvmjke iVhQiq"><div class="aw-1njknqq hYaBbk"><picture><source data-testid="source-for-S" media="(max-width: 767px)" srcSet="https://images.cdn.yle.fi/image/upload/ar_1.7777777910232544,c_fill,g_faces,h_431,w_767/dpr_2.0/q_auto:eco/f_auto/fl_lossy/13-3-7284665 768px)" srcSet="https://images.cdn.yle.fi/image/upload/ar_1.7777777910232544,c_fill,g_faces,h_357,w_636/dpr_2.0/q_auto:eco/f_auto/fl_lossy/13-3-7284665 2x,https://images.cdn.yle.fi/image/upload/ar_1.7777777910232544,c_fill,g_faces,h_357,w_636/dpr_1.0/q_auto:eco/f_auto/fl_lossy/13-3-7284665 1x"/><img alt="Tietoliikennejohtoja." src="https://images.cdn.yle.fi/image/upload/ar_1.7777777777777777,c_fill,g_faces,h_431,w_767/dpr_1.0/q_auto:eco/f_auto/fl_lossy/13-3-7284665" class="aw-1l9m598 hKVVvP"/></picture></div><div class="aw-45s348 dVgrWP"><button aria-disabled="false" aria-busy="false" class="ydscr__sc-17sr1bx-0 ydscr__sc-17sr1bx-2 fXVEol gbyyfi"><span class="ydscr__sc-17sr1bx-7 fdZgHS yds-button__content">Open image viewer</span></button></div></div></div><figcaption class="aw-kr26k0 ecbnKd"><span>Tietoturvayritys arvioi, että Turla on iskenyt yhteensä satoihin kohteisiin lähes viidessäkymmenessä maassa.</span><span> <!-- -->Image: Jyrki Lyytikkä / Yle</span></figcaption></figure><div class="aw-1hwlbbb dCDRiK"><div class="aw-kzjed4 dZqDYe yle__article__date"><time class="aw-lsqctp AmEBq yle__article__date--published" dateTime="2016-01-13T13:21:26+02:00">13.1.2016 13:21</time><span aria-hidden="true" class="aw-131q90r goLQmn">•</span><time class="aw-lsqctp AmEBq yle__article__date--modified" dateTime="2016-01-14T07:58:44+02:00">Updated<!-- --> <!-- -->14.1.2016 7:58</time></div></div></header><section class="yle__article__content"><p class="aw-1gybjub aw-1p7kakr cmIuaG fmSRng yle__article__paragraph">In 2013 Finland’s Foreign Ministry had its systems hacked by what investigators described as ‘a state actor’. Now Yle&#x27;s sources have confirmed who was behind the attack: the Turla group of Russian-speaking hackers who perpetrated attacks on targets in more than 50 countries worldwide during the same period.</p><p class="aw-1gybjub aw-1p7kakr cmIuaG fmSRng yle__article__paragraph">Stefan Tanase of Kaspersky security says that the Turla group is the premier Russian hacker organization—and it targets ministries, embassies and militaries in Russia’s neighbours. </p><p class="aw-1gybjub aw-1p7kakr cmIuaG fmSRng yle__article__paragraph">&quot;We believe that the Turla group is a nation state-sponsored attacker,&quot; said Tanase. &quot;We have seen traces in their malware and their servers, which we analyse, that point to the fact that the authors are Russian speaking and they definitely seem to have lot of resources to their cyber-espionage operation.&quot;</p><p class="aw-1gybjub aw-1p7kakr cmIuaG fmSRng yle__article__paragraph">Yle has confirmed from several European sources that the 2013 attacks on the Foreign Ministry were perpetrated by the Turla group. The Foreign Ministry says that it has investigated the attacks in the light of similar actions targeting other nation states around Russia.</p><p class="aw-1gybjub aw-1p7kakr cmIuaG fmSRng yle__article__paragraph">&quot;The typical signs in these attack tools can be observed once you get to the stage where you know what you’re looking for and can check to see if there’s anything like that, and if there have been any changes in their tools,&quot; said Ari Uusikartano of the Foreign Ministry.</p><p class="aw-1gybjub aw-1p7kakr cmIuaG fmSRng yle__article__paragraph">Uusikartano says that the attack by Turla hit most countries in western Europe. Kaspersky, which published a report on the methods and targets of Turla (which did not at the time mention Finland) last autumn, has outlined the methods used by the attackers.</p><p class="aw-1gybjub aw-1p7kakr cmIuaG fmSRng yle__article__paragraph">First, cyber spies start by gathering information about the target via sources like social media, public websites and internal phone directories.</p><p class="aw-1gybjub aw-1p7kakr cmIuaG fmSRng yle__article__paragraph">Second, they choose a few employees to whom they send emails which include a link to an apparently interesting website, which appears to be connected somehow to the targets everyday life or area of specialization. The hackers have however embedded malware in the site concerned.</p><p class="aw-1gybjub aw-1p7kakr cmIuaG fmSRng yle__article__paragraph">Third, when the employee visits the site, the malware ends up on his or her computer.</p><p class="aw-1gybjub aw-1p7kakr cmIuaG fmSRng yle__article__paragraph">That allows in the attacker, as happened to the Finnish Foreign Ministry in 2013. The ministry says it&#x27;s learned it&#x27;s lessons from this attack--but the hackers may already have moved on to a new method.</p></section></div><footer class="yle__article__footer"><div
